<div>   
<p style=";font-size: 14px;font-family: DengXian;white-space: normal"><br></p><p style="margin: 0 0 10px;font-size: 14px;font-family: DengXian;white-space: normal;text-indent: 25px;line-height: 25px;background-color: white"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">2021</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">年度</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">JCR</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">共收录科技期刊</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">9626</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">种，相比</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">2020</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">年度的</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">9500</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">种增加</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">126</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">种，增幅为</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">1.33%</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">。</span></p><p style="margin: 0 0 10px;font-size: 14px;font-family: DengXian;white-space: normal;text-indent: 25px;line-height: 25px;background-color: white"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">本年度中国大陆地区（</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">China Mainland</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">）计有</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">273</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">种期刊被收录，相比</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">2020</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">年度的</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">252</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">种增加</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">21</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">种，增幅为</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">8.33%</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">。</span></p><p style="margin: 0 0 10px;font-size: 14px;font-family: DengXian;white-space: normal;text-indent: 25px;line-height: 25px;background-color: white"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">从影响因子的学科分区看，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">2020</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">年度中国大陆地区期刊位列</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">Q1</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">区</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">(“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">期刊影响因子的学科相对排名</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">位列前</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">25%)</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">的期刊数量相对</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">2020</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">年度的</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">85</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">种上升至</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">123</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">种，占总数</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">273</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">种的</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">45.1%</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">Q2</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">区期刊</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">70</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">种，占总数</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">273</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">种的</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;color: #3333FF">25.6%</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #3333FF">。</span></p><p style="margin: 0 0 10px;font-size: 14px;font-family: DengXian;white-space: normal;text-indent: 25px;line-height: 25px;background-color: white"><strong><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: #333333">附：2021年度中国大陆SCI收录期刊主要文献计量指标</span></strong></p><p style=";font-size: 14px;font-family: DengXian;white-space: normal;text-indent: 24px;line-height: 20px;background-color: white"><span style="font-size: 12px;font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif">Total Cites-</span><span style="font-size: 12px;font-family: 宋体">总被引频次，</span><span style="font-size: 12px;font-family: 'Times New Roman',
